It is very powerful and super easy to use. It is fast and capable of loading huge models. It is a great tool for viewing, reviewing and collaborating on 3D assets.\r\n\r\n\r\nMajor Features:\r\n\r\nOpen 3D data file in IGES (.igs or .iges) format\r\n\r\nView models in 3D, spinning, panning, zooming in/out with perspective or orthographic projection\r\n\r\nMeasure distance, location, volume, area, length, radius, angle, boundary and many more\r\n\r\nSupport different rendering mode, support rendering color and background customization\r\n\r\nOpen multiple files in the same window so that you can compare 3D models\r\n\r\nExport in STL, DAE, DXF, OBJ, PLY and ATD formats\r\n\r\nDesigned for Microsoft Modern Style User Interface\r\n\r\nSupport both mouse and touch\r\n\r\nSupport opening 3D files from local drive, email attachments or One Drive\r\n\r\nProvide native zip/unzip support, support loading zipped 3D files directly\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\nThe app is part of ATView3D 3D visualization tool family developed by Afanche Technologies. ATView3D 3D visualization apps are widely used by professionals all over the world. If you need app for other 3D file formats, please search 'Afanche' to find more 3D apps.
